# Export RLum-objects to CSV

This function exports
[RLum](https://r-lum.github.io/Luminescence/reference/RLum-class.md)-objects
to CSV-files using the R function
[utils::write.table](https://rdrr.io/r/utils/write.table.html). All
[RLum](https://r-lum.github.io/Luminescence/reference/RLum-class.md)-objects
are supported, but the export is lossy, i.e. the pure numerical values
are exported only. Information that cannot be coerced to a
[data.frame](https://rdrr.io/r/base/data.frame.html) or a
[matrix](https://rdrr.io/r/base/matrix.html) are discarded as well as
metadata.

## Usage

``` r
write_RLum2CSV(
  object,
  path = NULL,
  prefix = "",
  export = TRUE,
  compact = TRUE,
  ...
)
```

## Arguments

- object:

  [RLum](https://r-lum.github.io/Luminescence/reference/RLum-class.md)
  or a [list](https://rdrr.io/r/base/list.html) of `RLum` objects
  (**required**): objects to be written. Can be a
  [data.frame](https://rdrr.io/r/base/data.frame.html) if needed
  internally.

- path:

  [character](https://rdrr.io/r/base/character.html) (*optional*):
  character string naming folder for the output to be written. If
  nothing is provided `path` will be set to the working directory.
  **Note:** this argument is ignored when `export = FALSE`.

- prefix:

  [character](https://rdrr.io/r/base/character.html) (*with default*):
  optional prefix to name the files. This prefix is valid for all
  written files

- export:

  [logical](https://rdrr.io/r/base/logical.html) (*with default*):
  enable/disable the file export. If set to `FALSE` nothing is written
  to the file connection, but a list comprising objects of type
  [data.frame](https://rdrr.io/r/base/data.frame.html) and
  [matrix](https://rdrr.io/r/base/matrix.html) is returned instead.

- compact:

  [logical](https://rdrr.io/r/base/logical.html) (*with default*): if
  `TRUE` (default) the output will be simpler but less comprehensive,
  that is not all elements in the objects will be fully broken down.
  This is in particular useful for writing `RLum.Results` objects to CSV
  files, as such objects can be rather complex and not all information
  are needed in a CSV file or can be meaningfully translated to CSV
  format.

- ...:

  further arguments that will be passed to the function
  [utils::write.table](https://rdrr.io/r/utils/write.table.html). All
  arguments except the argument `file` are supported

## Value

The function returns either a CSV-file (or many of them) or for the
option `export == FALSE` a list comprising objects of type
[data.frame](https://rdrr.io/r/base/data.frame.html) and
[matrix](https://rdrr.io/r/base/matrix.html)

## Details

However, in combination with the implemented import functions, nearly
every supported import data format can be exported to CSV-files, this
gives a great deal of freedom in terms of compatibility with other
tools.

**Input is a list of objects**

If the input is a [list](https://rdrr.io/r/base/list.html) of objects
all explicit function arguments can be provided as
[list](https://rdrr.io/r/base/list.html).

## Function version

0.2.2

## See also

[RLum.Analysis](https://r-lum.github.io/Luminescence/reference/RLum.Analysis-class.md),
[RLum.Data](https://r-lum.github.io/Luminescence/reference/RLum.Data-class.md),
[RLum.Results](https://r-lum.github.io/Luminescence/reference/RLum.Results-class.md),
[utils::write.table](https://rdrr.io/r/utils/write.table.html)

## Author

Sebastian Kreutzer, Geography & Earth Science, Aberystwyth University
(United Kingdom) , RLum Developer Team

Function version 0.2.2. In: Kreutzer, S., Burow, C., Dietze, M., Fuchs,
M.C., Schmidt, C., Fischer, M., Friedrich, J., Mercier, N., Philippe,
A., Riedesel, S., Autzen, M., Mittelstrass, D., Gray, H.J., Galharret,

Comprehensive Luminescence Dating Data Analysis. R package version
1.1.2. https://r-lum.github.io/Luminescence/

## Examples

``` r
## transform values to a list (and do not write)
data(ExampleData.BINfileData, envir = environment())
object <- Risoe.BINfileData2RLum.Analysis(CWOSL.SAR.Data)[[1]]
write_RLum2CSV(object, export = FALSE)
```
